<div id="review_1991245491" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1991245491" />
    <a title="Kendall" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/42327848-kendall"><img alt="Kendall" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1538940218p2/42327848.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1991245491?book_show_action=true">Oct 08, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kendall" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kendall" href="/user/show/42327848-kendall">Kendall</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42327848-kendall?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1991245491" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11619597988696439833">One thing that I admire about Colleen Hoover is her ability to write such beautiful, refreshing, and powerful novels! <br/><br/>Without Merit is nothing like her previous books that I have read. I would not classify this book as a romance at all (I mean maybe a little here and there). This to me would be a story about self discovery and finding your place in the world. This story is real, raw, beautiful, and painful at times. Hoover will steal your heart with this one.<br/><br/>Merit Voss comes from a very interest</span>
  <span id="freeText11619597988696439833" style="display:none">One thing that I admire about Colleen Hoover is her ability to write such beautiful, refreshing, and powerful novels! <br /><br />Without Merit is nothing like her previous books that I have read. I would not classify this book as a romance at all (I mean maybe a little here and there). This to me would be a story about self discovery and finding your place in the world. This story is real, raw, beautiful, and painful at times. Hoover will steal your heart with this one.<br /><br />Merit Voss comes from a very interesting and dysfunctional family (which I think most of us do have some dysfunctionality in our families whether you choose to admit it or not). <br /><br />"No one would be able to determine from the outside of our house that our family of seven includes an atheist, a home wrecker, an ex-wife suffering from a severe case of agoraphobia, <br />and a teenage girl whose weird obsession borders on necrophilia. <br />No one would be able to determine any of that from inside our house, either."<br /><br />Merit is a very unique and refreshing character. She is struggling with sadness and trying to fill a "void" that she can't quite figure out. Merit is a character that is very relatable to many of us. We all struggle with hard times, we have crazy and dysfunctional family members that we want to punch in the face at times, and live with the general ups/downs of life. <br /><br />This story is so powerful and has some many layers to it. The writing is absolutely brilliant! The story builds and builds and finally it all just comes tumbling down like a snowball effect. And YOU the reader are right there to witness it ALL. <br /><br />Merit is the keeper of secrets in the Voss household. A huge theme that enfolds in this novel is perspective. All of the members in this household each had a secret of their own that Merit has kept. But, sometimes secrets aren't always what they seem right? Perspective changes everything in this novel. You will keep coming back to this theme and ironically PERSPECTIVE is what made this NOVEL come ALIVE. I think we are all very quick to judge situations when we are not in them ourselves (even if it's not consciously). <br />"Not every mistake deserves a consequence. Sometimes the only thing it deserves is forgiveness." <br /> <br />This is an eye opener that holds such powerful messages about love, depression, grief, and sexuality. This is a strong and stellar read that I recommend to everyone. This is one of my favorite reads for 2017. I can't get enough of Hoover!!! :)</span>
  <a data-text-id="11619597988696439833" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2158698044" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2158698044" />
    <a title="Berit☀️✨" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/38946743-berit"><img alt="Berit☀️✨" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1534383878p2/38946743.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2158698044?book_show_action=true">Nov 26, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Berit☀️✨" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Berit☀️✨" href="/user/show/38946743-berit">Berit☀️✨</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook 9781508237129" href="/book/show/33347497-without-merit">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38946743-berit?shelf=favorite-author">favorite-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38946743-berit?shelf=audiobooks">audiobooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38946743-berit?shelf=2017">2017</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2158698044" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3944167298137970938"><b>5 spectacular stars! With MERIT!🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟</b><br/><br/>CoHo did it again!!! Last year the book that had the biggest impact on me was Colleen Hoover’s <i>It Ends With Us</i>.... that book still sticks with me today, it wrecked me, it hit me where I live, it was just simply perfection.... so I was a bit nervous to pick up this book, how could it possibly live up to my expectations? Well I’m happy to say it definitely did!!!<br/><br/>This book is different from any CoHo book I’ve read before..... but definitely in a good way.... thi</span>
  <span id="freeText3944167298137970938" style="display:none"><b>5 spectacular stars! With MERIT!🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟</b><br /><br />CoHo did it again!!! Last year the book that had the biggest impact on me was Colleen Hoover’s <i>It Ends With Us</i>.... that book still sticks with me today, it wrecked me, it hit me where I live, it was just simply perfection.... so I was a bit nervous to pick up this book, how could it possibly live up to my expectations? Well I’m happy to say it definitely did!!!<br /><br />This book is different from any CoHo book I’ve read before..... but definitely in a good way.... this book was about family, dysfunction, love, and secrets....<br /><br />Merit lives in a small Texas town and is certain her family is the most dysfunctional family ever.... and she may not be all that wrong, from the fact that they live in a renovated church with the marquee still on the lawn to the fact that both her stepmother and mother live in the same house..... Merit was such a fantastically developed character.... even if you couldn’t completely relate to her, you sure did want everything to work out for her.... she made me really think about the negative and positive side to having an identical twin (she had an identical twin Honor).... she also made me think about the burden of family secrets....<br /><br />This book touched on many difficult subjects.... but it was all done very subtly using all these wonderful characters who slowly reveal their secrets to us through Merit.... I also appreciated that there weren’t any clear answers given as to what everybody “needed“ To do to fix themselves..... The fix just simply began with letting go of secrets and learning to communicate..... this family has a ways to go, but I truly believe there is hope<br /><br />This character driven book definitely takes you on a rollercoaster of emotion and it is absolutely a ride I am thrilled I took! Highly recommend two fans of this author and anyone else who enjoys a book with amazing characters young or old!<br /><br />PS: there is a really adorable romance running through this book as well, it just kind of takes a backseat to the rest that is going on, but it is still super sweet💕</span>
  <a data-text-id="3944167298137970938" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2147849724" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2147849724" />
    <a title="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time"><img alt="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1365526640p2/13070326.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2147849724?book_show_action=true">Oct 08, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" href="/user/show/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time">Heather K (dentist in my spare time)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=hype-hype-hype">hype-hype-hype</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=m-f">m-f</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=beta-heros-in-mf">beta-heros-in-mf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=little-to-no-sex-content">little-to-no-sex-content</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=addiction-or-mental-disorders">addiction-or-mental-disorders</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2147849724" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6448799368107009112"><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5430144.Colleen_Hoover' title='Colleen Hoover' rel='nofollow noopener'>Colleen Hoover</a> is a very popular author, and it isn't hard to see why. I've hated as many of her books as I've liked, but there is something <b>compulsively readable</b> about her stories. I think if she gets anything right, it's her pacing, which is nearly always spot on. I can read one of her books for hours without getting bored. Angry, maybe, but not bored. <br/><br/><b>Trigger warnings: suicidal thoughts or tendencies, depression, and mental illness.</b><br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/33280872.Without_Merit' title='Without Merit by Colleen Hoover' rel='nofollow noopener'>Without Merit</a> is a <b>very busy book that tries to accomplish a </b></span>
  <span id="freeText6448799368107009112" style="display:none"><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5430144.Colleen_Hoover" title="Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Colleen Hoover</a> is a very popular author, and it isn't hard to see why. I've hated as many of her books as I've liked, but there is something <b>compulsively readable</b> about her stories. I think if she gets anything right, it's her pacing, which is nearly always spot on. I can read one of her books for hours without getting bored. Angry, maybe, but not bored. <br /><br /><b>Trigger warnings: suicidal thoughts or tendencies, depression, and mental illness.</b><br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/33280872.Without_Merit" title="Without Merit by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Without Merit</a> is a <b>very busy book that tries to accomplish a lot of things</b>. There is the set-up of how Merit is <i>so interesting</i> because she collects trophies and doesn't wear make up, and there is a promise of some big secrets (which there are a lot of, actually), but it feels like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5430144.Colleen_Hoover" title="Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Colleen Hoover</a> is really pushing this uber-quirky vibe to make her book different. Everything from the cast of characters with their outrageous names to the fact that they live in a converted church is made to make the book feel more unique, more "out there," for better or for worse. <br /><br /><b>There is too much going on with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/33280872.Without_Merit" title="Without Merit by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Without Merit</a> to make many of the messages effective.</b> And there are a lot of messages, some of them valid, some of them off the mark. Many are <i>after school special</i>-feeling, but many are somewhat impactful, even if the impact gets muted by the busy plotline filled with minor twists and turns. <br /><br />One thing I have to address is an issue that gets more or less swept under the rug and forgiven way too easily. I won't talk about it because I don't want to give away spoilers, but events like those that happened to Merit are extremely damaging and should not be forgiven in a simple conversation. I hated how Colleen Hoover made it seem like forgive and forget was the right thing to do in that situation. <br /><br />In terms of the characters, Sagan was too much of an angelic, can-do-no-wrong person, IMO. He was the "good one" in a field of more complex characters, and it irked me. <br /><br />I also didn't like how there was<b> so much miscommunication</b>. If there was just a minor amount of communication between any of the MCs, much of the drama would have been avoided and the book wouldn't have gotten on my nerves as much. I also agree with other reviewers about the <b>biphobia, slut-shaming, and lack of learning from mistakes/experiences.</b> I think this book is framed to be open-minded about mental illness and sexuality but it is anything but. <br /><br /><b>Overall, this book wasn't what I expected. It isn't a romance, but more of a family drama story with a love aspect thrown in. It is also very depressing and bleak, so know that going in. </b><br /><br />While it was more mature than some of the YA stuff I've seen from Hoover, I didn't quite enjoy it, and I'm frankly not pleased I paid full price for it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6448799368107009112" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Sometimes the only thing it deserves is forgiveness.<br>The Voss family is anything but normal. They live in a repurposed church, newly baptized Dollar Voss. The once cancer-stricken mother lives in the basement, the father is married to the mother’s former nurse, the little half-brother isn’t allowed to do or eat anything fun, and the eldest siblings are irritatingly perfect. Then, there’s Merit.<br>Merit Voss collects trophies she hasn’t earned and secrets her family forces her to keep. While browsing the local antiques shop for her next trophy, she finds Sagan. Merit retreats deeper into herself, watching her family from the sidelines when she learns a secret that no trophy in the world can fix.<br>Fed up with the lies, Merit decides to shatter the happy family illusion that she’s never been a part of before leaving them behind for good. When her escape plan fails, Merit is forced to deal with the staggering consequences of telling the truth and losing the one boy she loves.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="831425258198653268" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4514828-susanne-strong?shelf=library-book">library-book</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3123124374" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer16202183555604332978">4 Stars<br/><br/><b>A Coming of Age Novel about Life, Trials and Tribulations and Friendship</b><br/><br/>So what can I tell you about this CoHo novel? Again, it was totally unexpected. I have been kind of going in blind as of late with almost every book I read, that way all books are surprises. So yes, CoHo kind of has a style, but she also kind of doesn’t. None of her books are all that alike. Yes, some have romance in them, but lots aren’t entirely about that. Such is the case with “Without Merit”. <br/><br/>“Without Merit” is a</span>
  <span id="freeText16202183555604332978" style="display:none">4 Stars<br /><br /><b>A Coming of Age Novel about Life, Trials and Tribulations and Friendship</b><br /><br />So what can I tell you about this CoHo novel? Again, it was totally unexpected. I have been kind of going in blind as of late with almost every book I read, that way all books are surprises. So yes, CoHo kind of has a style, but she also kind of doesn’t. None of her books are all that alike. Yes, some have romance in them, but lots aren’t entirely about that. Such is the case with “Without Merit”. <br /><br />“Without Merit” is a coming of age novel about Seventeen year old Merit Voss, who lives at Dollar Voss (a/k/a a former church) with her entire family, including her twin sister Honor, her brothers, her father and step-mother and her mother (who lives in the basement). Life is far from perfect and communication is almost non-existent. <br /><br />For Merit, life is not easy and she has to figure out how to navigate the ins and outs, virtually alone. The moment she meets the eyes of a stranger in a vintage shop, it’s like a match is struck and the light never goes out. When he kisses her on a whim, she can’t resist. Disaster strikes when Merit finds out that “Sagan” is her twin sister’s new boyfriend!<br /><br /><b>What struck me listening to this is how CoHo always includes important, everyday issues in all of her novels. Issues that each of us encounter all of the time. The pertinent ones in “Without Merit” built slowly and I truly appreciated the way this novel drew me in.</b> Merit’s trial and tribulations pulled at me and I desperately wanted to help her. <b>This is one of my favorite of CoHo’s novels so far and I’m so glad that I’m continuing on the journey. </b><br /><br />Thanks to my local library for lending me a copy.<br /><br />Published on Goodreads on 1.12.20.</span>

<div id="review_2140424760" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2140424760" />
    <a title="Tweebs♥️ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/35431290-tweebs"><img alt="Tweebs♥️ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600454813p2/35431290.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2140424760?book_show_action=true">Oct 01, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tweebs♥️ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tweebs♥️ " href="/user/show/35431290-tweebs">Tweebs♥️ </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35431290-tweebs?shelf=books-that-killed-me-and-my-ghost">books-that-killed-me-and-my-ghost</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2140424760" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4925699573605853644"><b>
  <i>“Not every mistake deserves a consequence. Sometimes the only thing it deserves is forgiveness.” </i>
</b><br/><br/><i>{calls help line} </i><br/>person: how may I help you? <br/>me: i have lost the ability to even <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1506906992ra/24065463.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><u>THIS IS HOW YOU SPELL COLLEEN HOOVER: </u><br/><br/><b> Q U E E N </b> <br/><br/>She has done it again. She had zero mercy on my poor, smol heart. She ripped it into tiny little pieces by her<b> heartfelt, breathtaking plot, <i>"addictive like crack"</i> writing, and A+++++ characters.</b> She crushed me with feels like If I could sum up this book into one wor</span>
  <span id="freeText4925699573605853644" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“Not every mistake deserves a consequence. Sometimes the only thing it deserves is forgiveness.” </i>
</b><br><br><i>{calls help line} </i><br>person: how may I help you? <br>me: i have lost the ability to even <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1506906992ra/24065463.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>THIS IS HOW YOU SPELL COLLEEN HOOVER: </u><br><br><b> Q U E E N </b> <br><br>She has done it again. She had zero mercy on my poor, smol heart. She ripped it into tiny little pieces by her<b> heartfelt, breathtaking plot, <i>"addictive like crack"</i> writing, and A+++++ characters.</b> She crushed me with feels like If I could sum up this book into one word, it'd be <b>tears.</b> Why? It's all I've ever known since reading this book. Colleen Hoover, I'm coming over to your house with my tears because I just <i> hdfjhdskjghfdkjgfhdkjgfhdgkjf what is english??? i cannot english???</i> <br><br>Speaking of tears, I heard <s>from google</s> that 65% of your body is made up of water. <i>Mmmmm, interesting because….</i><br> <br><u><b>20% </b> </u>: wasted on the cover like <i>*slow claps*</i>, talk about aesthetics. I feel like whoever designed this, quite literally, went into my brain and took out everything I ever wanted for this cover. <br><br><u>
  <b>20% </b>
</u>: wasted from page 1 until the end of the book. Including, the acknowledgments too because it was a big reality check that the DAMN BOOK WAS OVER. <br><br><u><b>15% </b> </u>: wasted on the fact that I’m just an emotional human being, okay?? Anything sets me off. I should come with an attached warning. <i>Warning:</i> be gentle while handling. <br><br><u>
  <b>5% </b>
</u> : wasted over being disappointed that no one hasn’t invented a restart button. To be honest, how long do we have to wait? Until 3017? Because I want to read this again. <i>Now. </i><br><br><u>
  <b>5% </b>
</u> : Wtf is this water in my eyes ? Is there an onion near me? Am I crying AGAIN? God damn, my emotions are everywhere. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1506914313ra/24065853.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Anyway.</b><br><br>I had the pleasure of receiving this book a week before the official release date. I’m not even going to deny the fact that I did this as soon as the book was in my hands. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1506907887ra/24065531.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Listen, I couldn’t contain myself. It had to be done. I have no regrets. Okay, I lied. I totally regret screaming for 5 minutes straight. My throat didn't deserve this cruelty. In all honesty, I apologize if you're reading this entire review like, <i>"omg this is such a hot mess"</i>. Well, I'll be kind enough to provide y'all a <s>an excuse</s> translation for this whole thing. <br><br><u>Translation: </u><br><br><b>OH MY GOODNESS SOMEONE HOLD ME LIKE MY BODY WASN’T READY FOR THIS. </b><br><br> You have been warned but I'm 1000% y'all are going to be joining me in the, <i>"tears. tears everywhere" </i>, club. <br><br>I refuse to be alone in this. <br><br><b>Alright. </b><br><br>Where do I begin.....Where do I begin.....<br><br><b>In all seriousness. </b> You will find <i> depression, suicide, etc</i> within this book. I decided to add trigger warnings because everyone is different. Some people are perfectly okay with going into this book without knowing anything but other people may want to be prepared for what's in store for them. Don't worry, it's not the "focus" and makes you feel like the author went over board. I believe, y'all shouldn't know too much info about the plot because it's 3000 times better to watch it unravel. Makes the experience <b>way way WAY</b> better. Trust me, from one reader to another, i felt like this book hit me in the face and was like, <i>"listen you will love me or love me?" </i><br><br><b>Alrighty</b><br><br>No amount of words will be able to describe the eternal love I've developed for this book. I want to scream. I want to cry. Okay, why not both???? Like I said, ever since this book, I've been one tall glass of emotion. <b>Without Merit</b>, is going to be stored somewhere deep inside my heart. It's not like I had a choice. This book demanded to move inside my heart and was like, <i>"yo i'm just gonna live here". </i> <br><br><br><b>
  <i>"Don't make your presence known. Make your absence felt."</i>
</b><br><br><br>This is unlike anything I've ever read by Colleen Hoover. I've always known that she had this specialty to create phenomenal books that either make you never forget them or make you never forget them. This book was <b>intense, wild, mesmerizing, unique, and enjoyable. </b> It broke my heart in so many places. I can't even label what this book made me feel like. Maybe ask me in the next 3 years. <br><br><br><b>
  <i>"I'm not even sure home is a word that can be used to describe where I live. It's just a house filled with people who are counting down the days until they don't have to live with each other anymore." </i>
</b><br><br><br>What I can most definitely tell you with absolute certainty is that Colleen Hoover made me really look at things at a different perspective. She forced us to acknowledge the fact that there is individuals who deal with some of the issues being tackled within this book. It's <b>authentic, aching, and inspiring</b>; it's a damn good eye opener. <br><br><br><b>
  <i>"It’s incredible how much better a kiss can make you feel, right?”<br>I nod. “So incredible.”<br>His thumb brushes my cheek, then his satisfied grin falls into a pointed stare. “That’s exactly why I won’t do it again, Merit. You need to fall in love with yourself first.”</i>
</b><br><br><br>I felt the struggles, discarded feelings, worries, anguish, and fears. I found myself completely immersed and nodding at every fucking thing. I'm telling you, time will cease to exist and your only worry is flipping to the next page to find out what’s next.<br><br>I don't want to discuss the characters or anything about the plot. Not even the romance like oh my goodness I'm holding back soooooo much on that one. #ishipit #iloveit #yes #itsnoteventhemainfocus #anotheryes <br><br><br><b>
  <i>"Have you ever had one of their sugar cookies?" Sagan asks.<br>"Nope." I take a sip of my water.<br>"It'll change your life." He hands me the cookie and I take a bite. And then another. It really is the best cookie I've ever eaten, but he exaggerated.<br>"When is the life change supposed to happen, exactly? Do I have to eat the whole cookie to get the results?" <br>Sagan narrows his eyes at me. "Smartass," he says playfully." </i>
</b><br><br><br><i>I need a moment. Ahhhhhhhhhhhhh. </i><br> <br><b>All I will provide is : </b> This book will make you go through a roller coaster of endless feels. You will put this book down several times to just breathe. <i>AND I MEAN BREATHEEEEEE BECAUSE OH LORD HAVE MERCY WHAT IS AIR???</i> It will keep you on the edge like I forever found myself gripping my chair, my bag, a random stranger's hand, literally EVERYTHING WITHIN REACH.<br><br>This perfection called Without Merit will be out on October 3rd. Sorry for fangirling early but who could blame me? It was meant to be gushed upon and I simply couldn't hold myself back. I'll be lurking for updates on this book. And I'll slowly slide into your comment section and let out everything I've been holding back :) :) :) <br><br><br><b>
  <i>"I don’t matter here, either. If I dropped out of life, just like I dropped out of school, everyone’s lives would go on. With or without Merit."</i>
</b><br><br>Now, I'm going to kindly excuse myself and go hug the book while crying because god damn these tears won't end. <br><br><b>P.S: </b> Thank you <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5430144.Colleen_Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Colleen Hoover</a> for liking my review. You da bomb dot com &lt;3 <br><br><b>P.P.S: </b> God damn, you need to be sponsored by some Tissue company.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13556960081451146199"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479146098i/21153583.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>➦You know, sometimes while reading I keep thinking "Hey, I could totally write a story like that!" But I guess if I really REALLY wanted to, I could. Checklist, let's go:<br/><br/>✔spend ages on learning how to write without sounding like an imbecile<br/>✔come up with a somewhat decent romance story and characters<br/>✔hire an editor<br/>✔probably re-write the damn thing 100 times<br/>✔publish it anyways because I do what I want!<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413508472ra/11523228.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>➦What's the poi</span>
  <span id="freeText13556960081451146199" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479146098i/21153583.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>➦You know, sometimes while reading I keep thinking "Hey, I could totally write a story like that!" Provided that I could write. lol<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1508424885ra/24212278.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1508424885ra/24212279.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>➦I'm not implying that it's easy to write a book. But I guess if I really REALLY wanted to, I could. Checklist, let's go:<br><br>✔spend ages on learning how to write without sounding like an imbecile<br>✔come up with a somewhat decent romance story and characters<br>✔hire an editor<br>✔probably re-write the damn thing 100 times<br>✔publish it anyways because I do what I want!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413508472ra/11523228.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>➦What's the point of all this, you ask? I think anyone can write a book. A story that not only sends a powerful message, but that can also make you feel giddy at one moment and sad the next. <span id="freeTextContainer1942180737386559705">Colleen Hoover is one of my favorite authors and I have read almost every one of her books.<br/><br/>She is a <b>masterful storyteller</b>, not only does she captivates me with her stories but she manages to tackle difficult topics in an interesting and engaging way.<br/><br/><b>What is this book about?</b> Well, it's hard to describe because it's about so many things.   <span id="freeText1942180737386559705" style="display:none">Colleen Hoover is one of my favorite authors and I have read almost every one of her books.<br><br>She is a <b>masterful storyteller</b>, not only does she captivates me with her stories but she manages to tackle difficult topics in an interesting and engaging way.<br><br><b>What is this book about?</b> Well, it's hard to describe because it's about so many things. In the most simplistic form it's about Merit, a 17 year-old teenager with a twin sister. Merit lives with her family and there are issues that have not been handled well in the past. <br><br>I don't want to say anymore about it because I feel it would be a spoiler, there are twits and turns and I'll let you discover them.  <br><br>The novel is narrated by Merit and it is <b>heartbreaking, mesmerizing but most of all wonderful</b>. <br><br>This book can be categorized as YA, contemporary fiction and romance and is similar to books like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15717943.Hopeless__Hopeless___1_" title="Hopeless (Hopeless, #1) by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Hopeless</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/27362503.It_Ends_with_Us" title="It Ends with Us by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">It Ends with Us</a>. <br><br>Overall <b>I enjoyed this novel</b> and recommend it to all. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1507580050i/24129261._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_2148160238" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2148160238" />
    <a title="Jennifer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2473504-jennifer"><img alt="Jennifer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1394406877p2/2473504.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2148160238?book_show_action=true">Oct 09, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer" href="/user/show/2473504-jennifer">Jennifer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=listened-to-audiobook">listened-to-audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=read-2017">read-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=stand-alone-novel">stand-alone-novel</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2148160238" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16759195292569080859">★★½<br/>There will be readers who believe this book was written just for them...and they will be right. It will speak life, laughter, and validation into their very soul. It will let them know that there is no perfect family, that there are no right or wrong feelings, that they can disclose seemingly insurmountable truths and survive, that they can forgive and give second chances, but most importantly that they must fall in love with themselves before they can fall in love with another. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/33280872.Without_Merit' title='Without Merit by Colleen Hoover' rel='nofollow noopener'>Without Merit</a></span>
  <span id="freeText16759195292569080859" style="display:none">★★½<br />There will be readers who believe this book was written just for them...and they will be right. It will speak life, laughter, and validation into their very soul. It will let them know that there is no perfect family, that there are no right or wrong feelings, that they can disclose seemingly insurmountable truths and survive, that they can forgive and give second chances, but most importantly that they must fall in love with themselves before they can fall in love with another. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/33280872.Without_Merit" title="Without Merit by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Without Merit</a> holds important lessons for a fragile age group. <br /><br />Alas, I am not in that intended audience. The overwhelming amount of quirkiness worked against me and not for me. Between the character names and the over-the-top family dysfunction that was more like a PG-rated version of <a href="http://www.imdb.com/title/tt1586680/" rel="nofollow noopener">Shameless</a>, I identified the various messages intended but did not feel them in my heart which saddened me to no end. This is freakin' <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5430144.Colleen_Hoover" title="Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Colleen Hoover</a>! I should have <i>felt</i> something. Unfortunately, no spark of engagement in the storyline and no investment in the characters. Maybe the fault lies in my present-day mood/circumstances, professional background in the field of behavioral health, my expectations about the CoHo experience, my prep for this book involving re-reading other well-loved Colleen titles, who knows. Reading is subjective. I didn't like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/33280872.Without_Merit" title="Without Merit by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Without Merit</a> but a whole lot of other readers will, and that's OK.<br /><br />Note: In my perspective, the following elements are not clear in the marketing of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/33280872.Without_Merit" title="Without Merit by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">Without Merit</a> so please be aware: It is not a romance. It feels very young adult with a seventeen-year-old heroine. The book's theme is based in mental health issues with possible trigger warnings for those who deal with a mood disorder. (The characters' names are annoying.) <br /><br /><b>My favorite quote:</b><br /><i>“It annoys me when people try to convince other people that their anger or stress isn’t warranted if someone else in the world is worse off than them. It’s bullshit. Your emotions and reactions are valid. Don’t let anyone tell you any different. You’re the only one who feels them.”</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="16759195292569080859" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1847639538" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1847639538" />
    <a title="Nazanin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39893246-nazanin"><img alt="Nazanin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600407709p2/39893246.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1847639538?book_show_action=true">Oct 08, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nazanin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nazanin" href="/user/show/39893246-nazanin">Nazanin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39893246-nazanin?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39893246-nazanin?shelf=2017">2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39893246-nazanin?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39893246-nazanin?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1847639538" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10245598837433530764"><b>5 With Merit Stars</b><br/><br/><i>"NOT EVERY MISTAKE DESERVES A CONSEQUENCE. SOMETIMES THE ONLY THING IT DESERVES IS FORGIVENESS."</i><br/><br/>Well, where to begin!? Lets look at this cover a little more! I love it! This cover alone tell you about the story! I have a question, how/where Ms. Hoover learn to write such stories!! I thinks it’s in her blood, right!? I love, love her writing style! She writes in such a way that you want just keep reading! This story was like you don’t want it ends but at the same time you can’t </span>
  <span id="freeText10245598837433530764" style="display:none"><b>5 With Merit Stars</b><br /><br /><i>"NOT EVERY MISTAKE DESERVES A CONSEQUENCE. SOMETIMES THE ONLY THING IT DESERVES IS FORGIVENESS."</i><br /><br />Well, where to begin!? Lets look at this cover a little more! I love it! This cover alone tell you about the story! I have a question, how/where Ms. Hoover learn to write such stories!! I thinks it’s in her blood, right!? I love, love her writing style! She writes in such a way that you want just keep reading! This story was like you don’t want it ends but at the same time you can’t read it faster!<br /><br />I think the story wasn’t just about Merit, it was about her family, From her point of view. How she struggles with them and them with their own problems. That she keeps their secrets and somehow they affect on her own life. At first I hated her family and I had a right but when I read more and more my hatred became less and less. Yes, some of them did terrible things but still. Maybe it was because of the author’s writing that you can’t hate them anymore. This family is falling apart but every family has its own moments. How to deal with it, is important. My fave character in this story was Luck. I liked him so, so much! He was like a great friend to Merit. Yeah, he had his problems too but like I said at the end I couldn’t tell that I don’t like these characters. I liked even Merit’s father. At the beginning I thought of him as a jerk but at the end I could feel his love for his kids.<br /><br />The writing was amazing and the story-line was just perfect! It’s well-paced. Told in Merit’s POV, 1st person. It’s a stand-alone novel. I loved it and hope you enjoy it just like me!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10245598837433530764" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('5P9bHMQmB2+fxhFlC8GrY1/LDmIwJJKre5iWM+mOhoWXlJTUO3EMOZKnHTDua8CZoEQ7P0yi4dYsq00iTM2YwQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('REhpRJdlFkmPvXEGgPDX2WH/wEUwOakvap9rE0uaRhI3I6aMaDIdH4LcfVNlWrwjnnD1GEy/2lI9rLAC7tlYVg==')})
  }

Shakespeare wrote in Twelfth Night, “If music be the food of love, play on!” Music is most decidedly the food of love in this novel, and they do indeed play on -- right up until the end.  Maybe Someday was written with a definite target audience in mind. This book will appeal to older teens and young adults, particularly females. For others, it will appear somewhat similar to other love stories that they will have read in the past that deals with love triangles, and the pain, joy and complications that surround relationships. What sets it apart, however, is the unique approach that Colleen Hoover takes.  She has created a novel that incorporates music as an essential theme while, at the same time, her main male protagonist is deaf. It imbues the story with an interesting angle.
